\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ MEMORY\ ALLOCATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ By\ default,\ we\ use\ malloc\ and\ free\ for\ memory\ allocation.\ \ To\ override\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ memory\ allocation,\ before\ the\ implementation\ \#include,\ add\ a:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ STBIR\_MALLOC(size,user\_data)\ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ STBIR\_FREE(ptr,user\_data)\ \ \ ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Each\ resize\ makes\ exactly\ one\ call\ to\ malloc/free\ (unless\ you\ use\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ extended\ API\ where\ you\ can\ do\ one\ allocation\ for\ many\ resizes).\ Under}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ address\ sanitizer,\ we\ do\ separate\ allocations\ to\ find\ overread/writes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ PERFORMANCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ library\ was\ written\ with\ an\ emphasis\ on\ performance.\ When\ testing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ stb\_image\_resize\ with\ RGBA,\ the\ fastest\ mode\ is\ STBIR\_4CHANNEL\ with\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STBIR\_TYPE\_UINT8\ pixels\ and\ CLAMPed\ edges\ (which\ is\ what\ many\ other\ resize}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ libs\ do\ by\ default).\ Also,\ make\ sure\ SIMD\ is\ turned\ on\ of\ course\ (default\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ 64-\/bit\ targets).\ Avoid\ WRAP\ edge\ mode\ if\ you\ want\ the\ fastest\ speed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ library\ also\ comes\ with\ profiling\ built-\/in.\ If\ you\ define\ STBIR\_PROFILE,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ you\ can\ use\ the\ advanced\ API\ and\ get\ low-\/level\ profiling\ information\ by\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ calling\ stbir\_resize\_extended\_profile\_info()\ or\ stbir\_resize\_split\_profile\_info()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ after\ a\ resize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Most\ of\ the\ routines\ have\ optimized\ SSE2,\ AVX,\ NEON\ and\ WASM\ versions.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ On\ Microsoft\ compilers,\ we\ automatically\ turn\ on\ SIMD\ for\ 64-\/bit\ x64\ and\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ARM;\ for\ 32-\/bit\ x86\ and\ ARM,\ you\ select\ SIMD\ mode\ by\ defining\ STBIR\_SSE2\ or\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STBIR\_NEON.\ For\ AVX\ and\ AVX2,\ we\ auto-\/select\ it\ by\ detecting\ the\ /arch:AVX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ /arch:AVX2\ switches.\ You\ can\ also\ always\ manually\ turn\ SSE2,\ AVX\ or\ AVX2\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ support\ on\ by\ defining\ STBIR\_SSE2,\ STBIR\_AVX\ or\ STBIR\_AVX2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ On\ Linux,\ SSE2\ and\ Neon\ is\ on\ by\ default\ for\ 64-\/bit\ x64\ or\ ARM64.\ For\ 32-\/bit,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ we\ select\ x86\ SIMD\ mode\ by\ whether\ you\ have\ -\/msse2,\ -\/mavx\ or\ -\/mavx2\ enabled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ on\ the\ command\ line.\ For\ 32-\/bit\ ARM,\ you\ must\ pass\ -\/mfpu=neon-\/vfpv4\ for\ both}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ clang\ and\ GCC,\ but\ GCC\ also\ requires\ an\ additional\ -\/mfp16-\/format=ieee\ to\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ automatically\ enable\ NEON.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ On\ x86\ platforms,\ you\ can\ also\ define\ STBIR\_FP16C\ to\ turn\ on\ FP16C\ instructions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ converting\ back\ and\ forth\ to\ half-\/floats.\ This\ is\ autoselected\ when\ we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ are\ using\ AVX2.\ Clang\ and\ GCC\ also\ require\ the\ -\/mf16c\ switch.\ ARM\ always\ uses\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ built-\/in\ half\ float\ hardware\ NEON\ instructions.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ You\ can\ also\ tell\ us\ to\ use\ multiply-\/add\ instructions\ with\ STBIR\_USE\_FMA.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Because\ x86\ doesn't\ always\ have\ fma,\ we\ turn\ it\ off\ by\ default\ to\ maintain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ determinism\ across\ all\ platforms.\ If\ you\ don't\ care\ about\ non-\/FMA\ determinism}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ are\ willing\ to\ restrict\ yourself\ to\ more\ recent\ x86\ CPUs\ (around\ the\ AVX\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ timeframe),\ then\ fma\ will\ give\ you\ around\ a\ 15\%\ speedup.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ You\ can\ force\ off\ SIMD\ in\ all\ cases\ by\ defining\ STBIR\_NO\_SIMD.\ You\ can\ turn}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ off\ AVX\ or\ AVX2\ specifically\ with\ STBIR\_NO\_AVX\ or\ STBIR\_NO\_AVX2.\ AVX\ is\ 10\%}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ to\ 40\%\ faster,\ and\ AVX2\ is\ generally\ another\ 12\%.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ ALPHA\ CHANNEL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Most\ of\ the\ resizing\ functions\ provide\ the\ ability\ to\ control\ how\ the\ alpha\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ channel\ of\ an\ image\ is\ processed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ alpha\ represents\ transparency,\ it\ is\ important\ that\ when\ combining}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ colors\ with\ filtering,\ the\ pixels\ should\ not\ be\ treated\ equally;\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ should\ use\ a\ weighted\ average\ based\ on\ their\ alpha\ values.\ For\ example,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ a\ pixel\ is\ 1\%\ opaque\ bright\ green\ and\ another\ pixel\ is\ 99\%\ opaque}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ black\ and\ you\ average\ them,\ the\ average\ will\ be\ 50\%\ opaque,\ but\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ unweighted\ average\ and\ will\ be\ a\ middling\ green\ color,\ while\ the\ weighted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ average\ will\ be\ nearly\ black.\ This\ means\ the\ unweighted\ version\ introduced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ green\ energy\ that\ didn't\ exist\ in\ the\ source\ image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00134\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ (If\ you\ want\ to\ know\ why\ this\ makes\ sense,\ you\ can\ work\ out\ the\ math\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ following:\ consider\ what\ happens\ if\ you\ alpha\ composite\ a\ source\ image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ over\ a\ fixed\ color\ and\ then\ average\ the\ output,\ vs.\ if\ you\ average\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ source\ image\ pixels\ and\ then\ composite\ that\ over\ the\ same\ fixed\ color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Only\ the\ weighted\ average\ produces\ the\ same\ result\ as\ the\ ground\ truth}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ composite-\/then-\/average\ result.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Therefore,\ it\ is\ in\ general\ best\ to\ "{}alpha\ weight"{}\ the\ pixels\ when\ applying}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ filters\ to\ them.\ This\ essentially\ means\ multiplying\ the\ colors\ by\ the\ alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ values\ before\ combining\ them,\ and\ then\ dividing\ by\ the\ alpha\ value\ at\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00145\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ end.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00146\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ computer\ graphics\ industry\ introduced\ a\ technique\ called\ "{}premultiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ alpha"{}\ or\ "{}associated\ alpha"{}\ in\ which\ image\ colors\ are\ stored\ in\ image\ files}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ already\ multiplied\ by\ their\ alpha.\ This\ saves\ some\ math\ when\ compositing,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ also\ avoids\ the\ need\ to\ divide\ by\ the\ alpha\ at\ the\ end\ (which\ is\ quite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ inefficient).\ However,\ while\ premultiplied\ alpha\ is\ common\ in\ the\ movie\ CGI}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ industry,\ it\ is\ not\ commonplace\ in\ other\ industries\ like\ videogames,\ and\ most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ consumer\ file\ formats\ are\ generally\ expected\ to\ contain\ not-\/premultiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ colors.\ For\ example,\ Photoshop\ saves\ PNG\ files\ "{}unpremultiplied"{},\ and\ web}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ browsers\ like\ Chrome\ and\ Firefox\ expect\ PNG\ images\ to\ be\ unpremultiplied.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ there\ are\ three\ possibilities\ that\ might\ describe\ your\ image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ resize\ expectation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1.\ images\ are\ not\ premultiplied,\ alpha\ weighting\ is\ desired}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2.\ images\ are\ not\ premultiplied,\ alpha\ weighting\ is\ not\ desired}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 3.\ images\ are\ premultiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Both\ case\ \#2\ and\ case\ \#3\ require\ the\ exact\ same\ math:\ no\ alpha\ weighting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ should\ be\ applied\ or\ removed.\ Only\ case\ 1\ requires\ extra\ math\ operations;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ other\ two\ cases\ can\ be\ handled\ identically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ stb\_image\_resize\ expects\ case\ \#1\ by\ default,\ applying\ alpha\ weighting\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00169\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ images,\ expecting\ the\ input\ images\ to\ be\ unpremultiplied.\ This\ is\ what\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00170\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ COLOR+ALPHA\ buffer\ types\ tell\ the\ resizer\ to\ do.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00171\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00172\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ you\ use\ the\ pixel\ layouts\ STBIR\_RGBA,\ STBIR\_BGRA,\ STBIR\_ARGB,\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STBIR\_ABGR,\ STBIR\_RX,\ or\ STBIR\_XR\ you\ are\ telling\ us\ that\ the\ pixels\ are\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ non-\/premultiplied.\ In\ these\ cases,\ the\ resizer\ will\ alpha\ weight\ the\ colors\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00175\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ (effectively\ creating\ the\ premultiplied\ image),\ do\ the\ filtering,\ and\ then\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00176\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ convert\ back\ to\ non-\/premult\ on\ exit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00177\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00178\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ you\ use\ the\ pixel\ layouts\ STBIR\_RGBA\_PM,\ STBIR\_RGBA\_PM,\ STBIR\_RGBA\_PM,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00179\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STBIR\_RGBA\_PM,\ STBIR\_RX\_PM\ or\ STBIR\_XR\_PM,\ you\ are\ telling\ that\ the\ pixels\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00180\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ARE\ premultiplied.\ In\ this\ case,\ the\ resizer\ doesn't\ have\ to\ do\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00181\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ premultipling\ -\/\ it\ can\ filter\ directly\ on\ the\ input.\ This\ about\ twice\ as\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00182\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ fast\ as\ the\ non-\/premultiplied\ case,\ so\ it's\ the\ right\ option\ if\ your\ data\ is\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00183\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ already\ setup\ correctly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00184\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ you\ use\ the\ pixel\ layout\ STBIR\_4CHANNEL\ or\ STBIR\_2CHANNEL,\ you\ are\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ telling\ us\ that\ there\ is\ no\ channel\ that\ represents\ transparency;\ it\ may\ be\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ RGB\ and\ some\ unrelated\ fourth\ channel\ that\ has\ been\ stored\ in\ the\ alpha\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ channel,\ but\ it\ is\ actually\ not\ alpha.\ No\ special\ processing\ will\ be\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ performed.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00190\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ difference\ between\ the\ generic\ 4\ or\ 2\ channel\ layouts,\ and\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ specialized\ \_PM\ versions\ is\ with\ the\ \_PM\ versions\ you\ are\ telling\ us\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ data\ *is*\ alpha,\ just\ don't\ premultiply\ it.\ That's\ important\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ using\ SRGB\ pixel\ formats,\ we\ need\ to\ know\ where\ the\ alpha\ is,\ because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ it\ is\ converted\ linearly\ (rather\ than\ with\ the\ SRGB\ converters).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Because\ alpha\ weighting\ produces\ the\ same\ effect\ as\ premultiplying,\ you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ even\ have\ the\ option\ with\ non-\/premultiplied\ inputs\ to\ let\ the\ resizer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ produce\ a\ premultiplied\ output.\ Because\ the\ intially\ computed\ alpha-\/weighted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ output\ image\ is\ effectively\ premultiplied,\ this\ is\ actually\ more\ performant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ than\ the\ normal\ path\ which\ un-\/premultiplies\ the\ output\ image\ as\ a\ final\ step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00203\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Finally,\ when\ converting\ both\ in\ and\ out\ of\ non-\/premulitplied\ space\ (for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00204\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ example,\ when\ using\ STBIR\_RGBA),\ we\ go\ to\ somewhat\ heroic\ measures\ to\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00205\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ensure\ that\ areas\ with\ zero\ alpha\ value\ pixels\ get\ something\ reasonable\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ in\ the\ RGB\ values.\ If\ you\ don't\ care\ about\ the\ RGB\ values\ of\ zero\ alpha\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ pixels,\ you\ can\ call\ the\ stbir\_set\_non\_pm\_alpha\_speed\_over\_quality()\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ function\ -\/\ this\ runs\ a\ premultiplied\ resize\ about\ 25\%\ faster.\ That\ said,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ when\ you\ really\ care\ about\ speed,\ using\ premultiplied\ pixels\ for\ both\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ out\ (STBIR\_RGBA\_PM,\ etc)\ much\ faster\ than\ both\ of\ these\ premultiplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ options.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ PIXEL\ LAYOUT\ CONVERSION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ resizer\ can\ convert\ from\ some\ pixel\ layouts\ to\ others.\ When\ using\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00215\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ stbir\_set\_pixel\_layouts(),\ you\ can,\ for\ example,\ specify\ STBIR\_RGBA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00216\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ on\ input,\ and\ STBIR\_ARGB\ on\ output,\ and\ it\ will\ re-\/organize\ the\ channels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00217\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ during\ the\ resize.\ Currently,\ you\ can\ only\ convert\ between\ two\ pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00218\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ layouts\ with\ the\ same\ number\ of\ channels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00219\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00220\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ DETERMINISM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00221\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ We\ commit\ to\ being\ deterministic\ (from\ x64\ to\ ARM\ to\ scalar\ to\ SIMD,\ etc).\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00222\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ requires\ compiling\ with\ fast-\/math\ off\ (using\ at\ least\ /fp:precise).\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00223\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Also,\ you\ must\ turn\ off\ fp-\/contracting\ (which\ turns\ mult+adds\ into\ fmas)!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00224\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ We\ attempt\ to\ do\ this\ with\ pragmas,\ but\ with\ Clang,\ you\ usually\ want\ to\ add\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00225\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/ffp-\/contract=off\ to\ the\ command\ line\ as\ well.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00226\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00227\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ For\ 32-\/bit\ x86,\ you\ must\ use\ SSE\ and\ SSE2\ codegen\ for\ determinism.\ That\ is,\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00228\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ the\ scalar\ x87\ unit\ gets\ used\ at\ all,\ we\ immediately\ lose\ determinism.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00229\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ On\ Microsoft\ Visual\ Studio\ 2008\ and\ earlier,\ from\ what\ we\ can\ tell\ there\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00230\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ no\ way\ to\ be\ deterministic\ in\ 32-\/bit\ x86\ (some\ x87\ always\ leaks\ in,\ even\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00231\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ with\ fp:strict).\ On\ 32-\/bit\ x86\ GCC,\ determinism\ requires\ both\ -\/msse2\ and\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00232\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/fpmath=sse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00233\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00234\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ we\ will\ not\ be\ deterministic\ with\ float\ data\ containing\ NaNs\ -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00235\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ NaNs\ will\ propagate\ differently\ on\ different\ SIMD\ and\ platforms.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00236\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00237\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ you\ turn\ on\ STBIR\_USE\_FMA,\ then\ we\ will\ be\ deterministic\ with\ other\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00238\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ fma\ targets,\ but\ we\ will\ differ\ from\ non-\/fma\ targets\ (this\ is\ unavoidable,\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00239\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ because\ a\ fma\ isn't\ simply\ an\ add\ with\ a\ mult\ -\/\ it\ also\ introduces\ a\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00240\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ rounding\ difference\ compared\ to\ non-\/fma\ instruction\ sequences.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00241\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00242\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ FLOAT\ PIXEL\ FORMAT\ RANGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00243\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Any\ range\ of\ values\ can\ be\ used\ for\ the\ non-\/alpha\ float\ data\ that\ you\ pass\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00244\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ in\ (0\ to\ 1,\ -\/1\ to\ 1,\ whatever).\ However,\ if\ you\ are\ inputting\ float\ values\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00245\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ but\ *outputting*\ bytes\ or\ shorts,\ you\ must\ use\ a\ range\ of\ 0\ to\ 1\ so\ that\ we\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00246\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ scale\ back\ properly.\ The\ alpha\ channel\ must\ also\ be\ 0\ to\ 1\ for\ any\ format\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00247\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ that\ does\ premultiplication\ prior\ to\ resizing.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00248\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00249\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Note\ also\ that\ with\ float\ output,\ using\ filters\ with\ negative\ lobes,\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00250\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ output\ filtered\ values\ might\ go\ slightly\ out\ of\ range.\ You\ can\ define\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00251\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STBIR\_FLOAT\_LOW\_CLAMP\ and/or\ STBIR\_FLOAT\_HIGH\_CLAMP\ to\ specify\ the\ range\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00252\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ to\ clamp\ to\ on\ output,\ if\ that's\ important.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00253\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00254\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ MAX/MIN\ SCALE\ FACTORS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00255\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ input\ pixel\ resolutions\ are\ in\ integers,\ and\ we\ do\ the\ internal\ pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00256\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ resolution\ in\ size\_t\ sized\ integers.\ However,\ the\ scale\ ratio\ from\ input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00257\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ resolution\ to\ output\ resolution\ is\ calculated\ in\ float\ form.\ This\ means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00258\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ effective\ possible\ scale\ ratio\ is\ limited\ to\ 24\ bits\ (or\ 16\ million}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00259\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ to\ 1).\ As\ you\ get\ close\ to\ the\ size\ of\ the\ float\ resolution\ (again,\ 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00260\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ million\ pixels\ wide\ or\ high),\ you\ might\ start\ seeing\ float\ inaccuracy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00261\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ issues\ in\ general\ in\ the\ pipeline.\ If\ you\ have\ to\ do\ extreme\ resizes,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00262\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ you\ can\ usually\ do\ this\ is\ multiple\ stages\ (using\ float\ intermediate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00263\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ buffers).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00264\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00265\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ FLIPPED\ IMAGES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00266\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Stride\ is\ just\ the\ delta\ from\ one\ scanline\ to\ the\ next.\ This\ means\ you\ can\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00267\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ use\ a\ negative\ stride\ to\ handle\ inverted\ images\ (point\ to\ the\ final\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00268\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ scanline\ and\ use\ a\ negative\ stride).\ You\ can\ invert\ the\ input\ or\ output,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00269\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ using\ negative\ strides.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00270\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00271\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ DEFAULT\ FILTERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00272\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ For\ functions\ which\ don't\ provide\ explicit\ control\ over\ what\ filters\ to\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00273\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ use,\ you\ can\ change\ the\ compile-\/time\ defaults\ with:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00274\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00275\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ STBIR\_DEFAULT\_FILTER\_UPSAMPLE\ \ \ \ \ STBIR\_FILTER\_something}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00276\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ STBIR\_DEFAULT\_FILTER\_DOWNSAMPLE\ \ \ STBIR\_FILTER\_something}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00277\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00278\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ See\ stbir\_filter\ in\ the\ header-\/file\ section\ for\ the\ list\ of\ filters.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00279\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ NEW\ FILTERS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ A\ number\ of\ 1D\ filter\ kernels\ are\ supplied.\ For\ a\ list\ of\ supported\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00282\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ filters,\ see\ the\ stbir\_filter\ enum.\ You\ can\ install\ your\ own\ filters\ by\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00283\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ using\ the\ stbir\_set\_filter\_callbacks\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00284\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00285\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ PROGRESS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00286\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ For\ interactive\ use\ with\ slow\ resize\ operations,\ you\ can\ use\ the\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00287\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ scanline\ callbacks\ in\ the\ extended\ API.\ It\ would\ have\ to\ be\ a\ *very*\ large\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00288\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ image\ resample\ to\ need\ progress\ though\ -\/\ we're\ very\ fast.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00289\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00290\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ CEIL\ and\ FLOOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00291\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ In\ scalar\ mode,\ the\ only\ functions\ we\ use\ from\ math.h\ are\ ceilf\ and\ floorf,\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00292\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ but\ if\ you\ have\ your\ own\ versions,\ you\ can\ define\ the\ STBIR\_CEILF(v)\ and\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00293\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ STBIR\_FLOORF(v)\ macros\ and\ we'll\ use\ them\ instead.\ In\ SIMD,\ we\ just\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00294\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ our\ own\ versions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00295\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00296\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ ASSERT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00297\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Define\ STBIR\_ASSERT(boolval)\ to\ override\ assert()\ and\ not\ use\ assert.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00298\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00299\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ FUTURE\ TODOS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00300\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ \ For\ polyphase\ integral\ filters,\ we\ just\ memcpy\ the\ coeffs\ to\ dupe}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00301\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ them,\ but\ we\ should\ indirect\ and\ use\ the\ same\ coeff\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00302\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ \ Add\ pixel\ layout\ conversions\ for\ sensible\ different\ channel\ counts}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00305\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ for\ bad\ input/output\ buffer\ alignments\ and\ pitch?}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00309\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ of\ cache.\ Probably\ also\ something\ possible\ with\ alternating\ between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00310\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ scattering\ and\ gathering\ at\ high\ resize\ scales?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00311\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ Rewrite\ the\ coefficient\ generator\ to\ do\ many\ at\ once.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00312\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ AVX-\/512\ vertical\ kernels\ -\/\ worried\ about\ downclocking\ here.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00313\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ Convert\ the\ reincludes\ to\ macros\ when\ we\ know\ they\ aren't\ changing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00314\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ Experiment\ with\ pivoting\ the\ horizontal\ and\ always\ using\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00315\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ vertical\ filters\ (which\ are\ faster,\ but\ perhaps\ not\ enough\ to\ overcome}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00316\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ pivot\ cost\ and\ the\ extra\ memory\ touches).\ Need\ to\ buffer\ the\ whole}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00317\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ image\ so\ have\ to\ balance\ memory\ use.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{06630\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
